3ï¸âƒ£ COMPONENTES REACT â€” SLIDER DE PREÃ‡OS
========================================

### Regra de preÃ§os (centralizada)

```ts
export function calculatePricing(qty: number) {
  const referencePrice = 140;

  if (qty === 1) {
    return {
      total: 0,
      average: 0,
      savings: referencePrice,
    };
  }

  let total = 0;

  if (qty === 2) total = 80;
  else if (qty === 3) total = 195;
  else if (qty === 4) total = 300;
  else if (qty === 5) total = 387.5;
  else if (qty === 6) total = 462;
  else total = qty * 74; // teto mÃ­nimo progressivo

  const average = total / qty;
  const savings = qty * referencePrice - total;

  return { total, average, savings };
}
```

* * *

### Componente Slider

```tsx
import { useState } from "react";
import { calculatePricing } from "@/utils/pricing";

export function PricingSlider() {
  const [qty, setQty] = useState(1);
  const { total, average, savings } = calculatePricing(qty);

  return (
    <div className="pricing-box">
      <h3>Quantas aulas vocÃª quer fazer?</h3>

      <input
        type="range"
        min={1}
        max={10}
        value={qty}
        onChange={(e) => setQty(Number(e.target.value))}
      />

      <div className="pricing-result">
        <h4>{qty} aula{qty > 1 && "s"}</h4>

        {qty === 1 ? (
          <p><strong>Total: R$ 0</strong></p>
        ) : (
          <>
            <p>Total: <strong>R$ {total.toFixed(2)}</strong></p>
            <p>PreÃ§o por aula: R$ {average.toFixed(2)}</p>
            <p>Economia: R$ {savings.toFixed(2)}</p>
          </>
        )}

        <button>
          {qty === 1 ? "Agendar aula gratuita" : "Continuar com desconto"}
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

1ï¸âƒ£ SCHEMA DE BANCO DE DADOS (PRODUÃ‡ÃƒO-READY)

ğŸ§© Tabela: `lesson_feedback`
----------------------------

```sql
CREATE TABLE lesson_feedback (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),

  user_id UUID NOT NULL,
  instructor_id UUID NOT NULL,
  lesson_id UUID NOT NULL,

  -- Compliance
  instructor_identity_confirmed BOOLEAN,
  instructor_identity_uncertain BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,

  -- AvaliaÃ§Ã£o geral
  overall_rating SMALLINT CHECK (overall_rating BETWEEN 1 AND 5),

  -- Qualidade da aula
  didactic_quality SMALLINT CHECK (didactic_quality BETWEEN 1 AND 5),
  politeness SMALLINT CHECK (politeness BETWEEN 1 AND 5),
  clarity SMALLINT CHECK (clarity BETWEEN 1 AND 5),
  vehicle_condition SMALLINT CHECK (vehicle_condition BETWEEN 1 AND 5),

  -- Estado emocional
  emotional_state VARCHAR(20)
    CHECK (emotional_state IN ('calm', 'slightly_nervous', 'nervous', 'very_nervous')),

  -- Causas do nervosismo
  nervous_reasons TEXT[], -- array
  nervous_other_reason TEXT,

  -- PreferÃªncias de apoio
  wants_breathing_exercises BOOLEAN,
  wants_confidence_tips BOOLEAN,
  wants_reminders BOOLEAN,

  -- ComentÃ¡rio livre
  comment TEXT,

  -- BÃ´nus
  bonus_eligible BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  bonus_paid BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  bonus_amount_cents INTEGER DEFAULT 0,

  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT now()
);
```

ğŸ§© Tabela: `final_feedback` (apÃ³s todas as aulas)

```sql

  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),

  user_id UUID NOT NULL,
  instructor_id UUID,

  confidence_level VARCHAR(20)

  would_repeat_instructor BOOLEAN,
  would_recommend_instructor BOOLEAN,

  helpful_features TEXT[], -- ex: ['ia_tutor', 'breathing', 'flex_schedule']

  improvement_suggestions TEXT,

  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT now()
);
```
